ltm rule /Common/aws-dns-proxy {
when CLIENT_ACCEPTED {
if { [class match [IP::client_addr] equals NRT-IB-IPs ] && [active_members NETENG-AP-NORTHEAST-1-ROUTE53-INBOUNDENDPOINTS-53] > 0 } {
 pool NETENG-AP-NORTHEAST-1-ROUTE53-INBOUNDENDPOINTS-53 }
elseif { [class match [IP::client_addr] equals NRT-IB-IPs] && [active_members NETENG-AP-SOUTHEAST-2-ROUTE53-INBOUNDENDPOINTS-53] > 0} {
 pool NETENG-AP-SOUTHEAST-2-ROUTE53-INBOUNDENDPOINTS-53 }
elseif { [class match [IP::client_addr] equals SYD-IB-IPs ] && [active_members NETENG-AP-SOUTHEAST-2-ROUTE53-INBOUNDENDPOINTS-53] > 0} {
pool NETENG-AP-SOUTHEAST-2-ROUTE53-INBOUNDENDPOINTS-53 }
elseif { [class match [IP::client_addr] equals SYD-IB-IPs ] && [active_members NETENG-AP-NORTHEAST-1-ROUTE53-INBOUNDENDPOINTS-53] > 0} {
pool NETENG-AP-NORTHEAST-1-ROUTE53-INBOUNDENDPOINTS-53 }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-blockhiddencontent {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    if { [HTTP::uri] contains "\/\." } {
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Contains Dot"
        HTTP::respond 200 "Connection" "close" "Blocked" "true"
        TCP::close
    }

    switch -glob [string tolower [HTTP::uri]] {
        *cmd.exe* -
        *telnet.exe* -
        *root.exe* -
        *ping.exe* -
        *awstats.pl?* {
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Contains some .exe"
        HTTP::respond 405
        discard
        }
    }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-cookies-secureflag {
when HTTP_RESPONSE {
   if {[HTTP::header exists "Set-Cookie"]}{  
        set count 0   
         foreach aheader [HTTP::header values "Set-Cookie"] { 

                # Removes headers on the first iteration of the loop
                # This way cookie headers are not doubled up
                        if {$count equals 0}
                        {
                                HTTP::header remove "Set-Cookie" 
                                incr {count}
                        }

                        # The following statements set cookies based on the attributes
                        # that are already present or lacking..... 

                        if {not(([string tolower $aheader] contains "; secure") || ([string tolower $aheader] contains ";secure"))} {
                                HTTP::header insert Set-Cookie "$aheader; secure"
                        } else {
                                HTTP::header insert Set-Cookie "$aheader"

                        }
      }
   }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-headers-remove {
when RULE_INIT {
        # Create a list of the response headers to delete.  
        set static::headers_to_delete [list x-fdsa-node x-fdsa-pid x-fdsa-stats-ttfbw \
x-powered-by x-aspnet-version server factset-redirector-cluster-affinity \
        factset-redirector-host factset-redirector-thread fds-node fds-pid fds-stats-ttfbw
        ]

        # Log debug messages to /var/log/ltm?  1=yes, 0=no.
        set static::clocking_debug 0
}

when HTTP_REQUEST {
  set HTTP_URI [HTTP::uri]
  set HTTP_HOST [HTTP::host]
}

when HTTP_RESPONSE {
        # Remove all headers in the delete list
        foreach aHeader [HTTP::header names] {
                if {[matchclass $static::headers_to_delete equals [string tolower $aHeader]]}{
                        while {[HTTP::header exists $aHeader]}{
                           if {$static::clocking_debug} {
                                log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:$HTTP_HOST, URI:$HTTP_URI, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Removing $aHeader: [HTTP::header value $aHeader]"
                        }
                                HTTP::header remove $aHeader
                        }
                }
        }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/log_http_headers_rule {
when CLIENT_ACCEPTED {
    set clientAccept 0
    set Httpreq 0
    set hsl [HSL::open -publisher /Common/publisher-remote-syslog]
    set CONNECTION_RECEIVE [clock clicks -milliseconds]
    set clientAccept 1
    #HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]"

}
when HTTP_REQUEST {
   set HTTP_REQUEST_RECEIVE [clock clicks -milliseconds]
   set myHost [HTTP::host]
   set myPath [HTTP::path]
   set myMethod [HTTP::method]
   #HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]"
   if {$clientAccept == 1 && $Httpreq == 0} { set Httpreq 1 }
   else
   { set clientAccept 0 }
   #HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]"

}
when HTTP_RESPONSE {
   set HTTP_RESPONSE_RECEIVE [expr {[clock clicks -milliseconds] - $HTTP_REQUEST_RECEIVE }]
   set CONNECTION_RESPONSE_RECEIVE [expr {[clock clicks -milliseconds] - $CONNECTION_RECEIVE}]
   set myConnect [HTTP::header Connection]
   set myStatus [HTTP::status]
   if {$clientAccept == 1}{HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port] [IP::server_addr]:[TCP::server_port] $myMethod $myPath \"[clock format [clock seconds] -format "%a, %d %h %Y %T"]\" $myHost $HTTP_RESPONSE_RECEIVE  total_time $CONNECTION_RESPONSE_RECEIVE $myConnect $myStatus"}
   else {HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port] [IP::server_addr]:[TCP::server_port] $myMethod $myPath \"[clock format [clock seconds] -format "%a, %d %h %Y %T"]\" $myHost $HTTP_RESPONSE_RECEIVE total_time 0  $myConnect $myStatus"}}
}
ltm rule /Common/rule-http-response-remove-keepalive {
#https://cdn.f5.com/product/bugtracker/ID714372.html
when HTTP_RESPONSE_RELEASE {
    HTTP::header remove keep-alive
}
}
ltm rule /Common/rule-http-version-identifier {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
  if { [HTTP2::active] } {
    HTTP::header insert X-http-ver h2
  } else {
    HTTP::header insert X-http-ver h1
  }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/rule-http-xfp-header-insert {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
  if { [TCP::local_port] == "80" } {
    HTTP::header insert X-Forwarded-Proto http
  } elseif { [TCP::local_port] == "443" } {
    HTTP::header insert X-Forwarded-Proto https
  }
}
}

ltm profile client-ssl /Common/SSL-FACTSET-CUSTOM {
    alert-timeout 60
    app-service none
    cert /Common/default.crt
    cert-key-chain {
        default {
            cert /Common/default.crt
            key /Common/default.key
        }
    }
    chain none
    cipher-group none
    ciphers ECDHE+AES-GCM:ECDHE+AES:RSA+AES-GCM:RSA+AES:-ADH:-EXP:-SSLv3:-TLSv1
    defaults-from /Common/clientssl
    handshake-timeout 60
    inherit-ca-certkeychain true
    inherit-certkeychain false
    key /Common/default.key
    options { no-tlsv1.3 no-sslv3 no-tlsv1 }
    passphrase none
    renegotiate-max-record-delay 10
    renegotiation disabled
}

#use the key in the default place: /config/rndc.key
 
controls {
    inet 127.0.0.1 port 953 allow {
        127.0.0.1;
    };
};
 
logging {
    channel logfile {
        syslog daemon;
        severity error;
        print-category yes;
        print-severity yes;
        print-time yes;
    };
    category default {
        logfile;
    };
    category config {
        logfile;
    };
    category notify {
        logfile;
    };
};
 
options {
    listen-on port 53 {
        127.0.0.1;
        "zrd-acl-000-000";
    };
    listen-on-v6 port 53 {
        ::1;
        fc00:f5::1;
        fe80::298:76ff:fe54:3210;
    };
    recursion no;
    directory "/config/namedb";
    allow-transfer {
        localhost;
    };
    check-names master warn;
     
    check-integrity yes;
    max-journal-size 1M;
    version "none";
    forwarders {
    };
};
 
acl "zrd-acl-000-000" {
    127.10.0.0;
};
 
view "external" {
    match-clients {
        "zrd-acl-000-000";
        any;
    };
};
